add_namespace = ww1_china

# YUAN EMPEROR
##################
country_event = {
	title = ww1_china.1.t
	desc = ww1_china.1.d
	id = ww1_china.1
	picture = GFX_report_event_chi_yuan_cabinet
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.1.a
		set_global_flag = chinese_warlord_crisis
		activate_mission_tooltip = CHI_warlord_era_mission
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_idea = CHI_idea_good_army_support
						has_idea = CHI_idea_good_popular_support
					}
					AND = {
						has_idea = CHI_idea_improved_army_support
						has_idea = CHI_idea_improved_popular_support
					}
					AND = {
						has_idea = CHI_idea_good_army_support
						has_idea = CHI_idea_improved_popular_support
					}
					AND = {
						has_idea = CHI_idea_improved_army_support
						has_idea = CHI_idea_good_popular_support
					}
				}
			}
			add_country_leader_trait = CHI_trait_accepted_monarch
		}
		else = {
			add_country_leader_trait = unpopular_monarch
		}
	}
}

#WARLORD ERA BEGINS - YUNNAN
##################
country_event = {
	title = ww1_china.2.t
	desc = ww1_china.2.d
	id = ww1_china.2
	picture = GFX_report_event_manchukuo_army
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = CHI
			tag = QIN
		}
		has_global_flag = warlord_era
		YUN = {
			exists = no
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			YUN = {
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_china_or_warlord = yes
					}
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								state = 325
							}
						}
						add_core_of = YUN
						YUN = {
							transfer_state = PREV
						}
					}
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					set_demilitarized_zone = no
				}
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = {
						has_character = CHI_tang_jiyao
					}
					CHI_tang_jiyao = {
						set_nationality = YUN
					}
				}
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = {
						has_character = CHI_cai_e
					}
					CHI_cai_e = {
						set_nationality = YUN
					}
				}
				CHI_tang_jiyao = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy }
						promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = {
								ideology = authoritarian_democracy
								traits = { chinese_federalist }
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = conservatism }
						promote_character = conservatism
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = {
								ideology = conservatism
								traits = { chinese_federalist }
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = stratocracy }
						promote_character = stratocracy
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = {
								ideology = stratocracy
							}
						}
					}
				}
				load_oob = CHI_warlord
				capital_scope = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"JuntuÃ¡n\"	start_experience_factor = 0.4	start_equipment_factor = 1"
						owner = PREV
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						count = 6
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_global_flag = cai_e_dead }
					}
					CHI_cai_e = {
						if = {
							limit = { has_ideology = revolutionary_nationalism }
							promote_character = revolutionary_nationalism
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								country_leader = {
									ideology = revolutionary_nationalism
									traits = {
										revolutionary_general
										generallissimo
									}
								}	
								promote_leader = yes
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy }
							promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								country_leader = {
									ideology = authoritarian_democracy
									traits = {
										revolutionary_general
										generallissimo
									}
								}	
								promote_leader = yes
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = { is_field_marshal = no }
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = QIN
					}
					inherit_technology = QIN
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 5000
						producer = QIN
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_tech = tech_support
						}
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = support_equipment
							amount = 500
							producer = QIN
						}
					}
					QIN = {
						add_to_faction = PREV
					}
					else = {
						inherit_technology = CHI
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = infantry_equipment
							amount = 5000
							producer = CHI
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_tech = tech_support
							}
							add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
								type = support_equipment
								amount = 500
								producer = CHI
							}
						}
						CHI = {
							set_truce = {
								target = PREV
								days = 330
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.2.a
	}
}

# REPUBLICAN PLOT (SECOND REVOLUTION)
########################################
country_event = {
	title = ww1_china.3.t
	desc = ww1_china.3.d
	id = ww1_china.3
	picture = GFX_report_event_manchukuo_army
	# fire_only_once = yes
	# trigger = {
	# 	tag = CHI
	# 	has_civil_war = no
	# 	has_idea = CHI_idea_republican_plot
	# 	NOT = {
	# 		has_government = democratic
	# 		has_completed_focus = CHI_second_empire
	# 		has_character = CHI_song_jiaoren
	# 		has_country_flag = republican_plot_fired
	# 	}
	# 	OR = {
	# 		democratic > 0.35
	# 		AND = {
	# 			democratic > 0.15
	# 			date > 1913.7.1
	# 		}
	# 	}
	# }
	# mean_time_to_happen = {
	# 	days = 7
	# }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.3.a
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = ww1_china.36 hours = 6 }
			# check_democratic_civil_war_popularity = yes
		}
		start_civil_war = {
			ideology = democratic
			size = 0.20
			states = {
				591
				592
				593
				594
				595
				598
				600
				602
				606
				613
				892
				893
			}
			keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
				OR = {
					is_character = CHI_cai_e # Cai E
					NOT = { has_trait = chinese_nationalist }
				}
			}
			keep_political_party_members = yes
			set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_uprising
			set_capital = {
				state = 598
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = chinese_second_revolution
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = -0.15
			}
			CHI_sun_yatsen = {
				set_nationality = CHR
			}
			CHI_hu_hanmin = {
				set_nationality = CHR
			}
			CHI_huang_xing = {
				set_nationality = CHR
			}
			CHR = {
				CHI_hu_hanmin = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = tridemism }
						promote_character = tridemism
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								ideology = tridemism
								traits = { conservative_nationalist }
							}
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
				CHI_sun_yatsen = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = tridemism }
						promote_character = tridemism
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								ideology = tridemism
								traits = { chinese_nationalist father_of_the_republic }
							}
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
				load_focus_tree = {
					tree = china_focus
					keep_completed = yes
				}
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = CHI_ruling_of_yuan_shikai
					uncomplete_children = yes
				}
				unlock_national_focus = CHI_kuomintang
				unlock_national_focus = CHI_three_principles
				unlock_national_focus = CHI_unite_opposition #cause they are already there
				mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
				add_ideas = CHI_idea_three_principles
				if = {
					limit = {
						PREV = {
							owns_state = 605
						}
					}
					set_province_controller = 10822
					set_province_controller = 10304
					set_province_controller = 4041
					set_province_controller = 11865
					set_province_controller = 10144
					set_province_controller = 5048
					set_province_controller = 2030
					set_province_controller = 1893
					set_province_controller = 4141
					set_province_controller = 2091
					set_province_controller = 12274
					set_province_controller = 8026
					set_province_controller = 7240
					set_province_controller = 6999
					set_province_controller = 4431
					set_province_controller = 7256
					set_province_controller = 12767
					set_province_controller = 1367
					set_province_controller = 4925
					set_province_controller = 1395
					set_province_controller = 12705
				}
			}
			set_capital = {
				state = 608
			}
		}
	}
}

# MILITARIST PLOT - Beiyang Coup
####################################
country_event = {
	title = ww1_china.4.t
	desc = ww1_china.4.d
	id = ww1_china.4
	picture = GFX_report_event_manchukuo_army
	# fire_only_once = yes
	# trigger = {
	# 	tag = CHI
	# 	has_civil_war = no
	# 	has_idea = CHI_idea_militarist_plot
	# 	NOT = {
	# 		has_government = fascism
	# 	}
	# 	NOT = {
	# 		has_completed_focus = CHI_suppress_monarchists
	# 	}
	# 	NOT = {
	# 		has_war_with = QIN
	# 	}
	# 	fascism > 0.35
	# }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	# mean_time_to_happen = {
	# 	days = 7
	# }
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.4.a
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = ww1_china.36 hours = 6 }
		}
		# triggering national protection war
		# if = {
		# 	limit = { has_global_flag = yuan_shikai_dead }
		# 	hidden_effect = {
		# 		unlock_national_focus = CHI_suppress_monarchists
		# 		set_global_flag = chinese_warlord_crisis
		# 		set_global_flag = national_protection_war
		# 		country_event = {
		# 			id = ww1_china.37
		# 		}
		# 	}
		# 	custom_effect_tooltip = ww1_china.4.a.tt
		# }
		check_neutrality_civil_war_popularity = yes
		start_civil_war = {
			ideology = fascism
			size = civil_war_size_var
			states = all
			states_filter = {
				is_capital = no
				NOT = { region = 165 }
			}
			keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = chinese_nationalist
					has_trait = chinese_federalist
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = CHI
					has_government = fascism
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_uprising
				load_focus_tree = {
					tree = china_focus
					keep_completed = yes
				}
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = CHI_kuomintang
					uncomplete_children = yes
				}
				unlock_national_focus = CHI_ruling_of_yuan_shikai
				mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
				remove_ideas = CHI_idea_support_for_revolution
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					long_name = CHI_neutrality_party
					name = CHI_neutrality_party
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
				set_popularities = {
					fascism = 31
					communism = 0
					democratic = 12
					neutrality = 57
				}
				set_capital = { state = 608 }
				ROOT = {
					every_unit_leader = {
						limit = {
							has_trait = CHI_loyalist
						}
						set_nationality = PREV.PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.4.b
		# yuan shikai couped the government
		hidden_effect = {
			uncomplete_national_focus = {
				focus = CHI_kuomintang
				uncomplete_children = yes
			}
			unlock_national_focus = CHI_ruling_of_yuan_shikai
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
			}
		}
		remove_ideas = CHI_idea_support_for_revolution
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			long_name = CHI_neutrality_party
			name = CHI_neutrality_party
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			promote_character = CHI_yuan_shikai
		}
		set_capital = { state = 608 }
		hidden_effect = {
			CHI_yuan_shikai = {
				promote_character = {
					ideology = oligarchism
				}
				promote_character = {
					ideology = stratocracy
				}
			}
			set_capital = {
				state = 608
			}
			set_popularities = {
				fascism = 25
				communism = 0
				democratic = 28
				neutrality = 47
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_song_jiaoren
				}
				country_event = {
					id = ww1_china.177
					days = 20
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 1000
				democratic < 0.20
			}
		}
	}
}

# SUN YUT-SEN AUTHORITARISM
##################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.6
	title = ww1_china.6.t
	desc = {
		text = ww1_china.6.d
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = yuan_shikai_dead
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ww1_china.6.d_yuan
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = yuan_shikai_dead }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_mountain
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.6.a
		set_global_flag = chinese_warlord_crisis
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = yuan_shikai_dead } }
			CHI_yuan_shikai = {
				remove_unit_leader_role = yes
				remove_country_leader_role = {
					ideology = stratocracy
				}
				remove_country_leader_role = {
					ideology = oligarchism
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#HIDDEN - HYPERINFLATION 70 DAYS PROGRAMM
##################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.7
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = CHI_land_reform
				}
				NOT = {
					has_idea = CHI_idea_inflation3
				}
			}
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_inflation3
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = CHI_land_reform
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = CHI_pay_off_debts
				}
				NOT = {
					has_idea = CHI_idea_inflation
				}
			}
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_inflation
		}
	}
}

# CRUSH MANCHU RESTORATION
##################
country_event = {
	title = ww1_china.8.t
	desc = ww1_china.8.d
	id = ww1_china.8
	picture = GFX_report_event_japan_army_mountainside
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = manchu_restoration
			CHI_duan_qirui = {
				promote_character = oligarchism
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_vice_president
				add_idea = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_president
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = neutrality
				long_name = CHI_neutrality_anfu_party
				name = CHI_neutrality_anfu_party
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.8.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = historical_tt
		QIN_zhang_xun = {
			set_nationality = QIN
			promote_leader = yes
		}
		set_global_flag = QIN_flag_manchu_rest_not_done
		QIN = {
			transfer_state = 608
			hidden_effect = {
				QIN_zhang_xun = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = oligarchism
							traits = {
								chinese_royalist generallissimo
							}
						}
					}
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = stratocracy
							traits = {
								chinese_royalist generallissimo
							}
						}
					}
				}
				set_province_controller = 2999
				set_province_controller = 9776
				CHI = {
					set_province_controller = 6828
					set_province_controller = 6828
					set_province_controller = 10068
					set_province_controller = 4137
					set_province_controller = 9969
					set_province_controller = 1134
					set_province_controller = 12026
				}
				QIN_end_japanese_concession = yes
				QIN_end_american_concession = yes
				QIN_end_italian_concession = yes
				QIN_end_russian_concession = yes
				QIN_end_french_concession = yes
				QIN_end_british_concession = yes
				QIN_end_german_concession = yes
				remove_ideas = QIN_idea_tongmenghui
				remove_ideas = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_2
				remove_ideas = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_3
				remove_ideas = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_4
				remove_ideas = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_5
				remove_ideas = QIN_idea_beiyang_army
				
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = neutrality
					long_name = QIN_neutrality_restoration_party_long
					name = QIN_neutrality_restoration_party
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_war_support = 0.40
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = CHI
					}
					add_core_of = QIN
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_claimed_by = CHI
					}
					add_claim_by = QIN
				}
				load_oob = "QIN_restoration"
				set_rule = {
					can_join_factions = no
				}
				add_ideas = standing_alone	
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = CHI
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.8.b
		QIN_zhang_xun = {
			set_nationality = QIN
			promote_leader = yes
		}		
		
		
		set_global_flag = QIN_flag_manchu_rest_not_done
		
		QIN = {
			transfer_state = 608
			hidden_effect = {
				set_province_controller = 2999
				set_province_controller = 9776
				CHI = {
					set_province_controller = 6828
					set_province_controller = 6828
					set_province_controller = 10068
					set_province_controller = 4137
					set_province_controller = 9969
					set_province_controller = 1134
					set_province_controller = 12026
				}
				QIN_end_japanese_concession = yes
				QIN_end_american_concession = yes
				QIN_end_italian_concession = yes
				QIN_end_russian_concession = yes
				QIN_end_french_concession = yes
				QIN_end_british_concession = yes
				QIN_end_german_concession = yes
				remove_ideas = QIN_idea_tongmenghui
				remove_ideas = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_2
				remove_ideas = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_3
				remove_ideas = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_4
				remove_ideas = QIN_idea_tongmenghui_5
				remove_ideas = QIN_idea_beiyang_army
				
				QIN_zhang_xun = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = oligarchism
							traits = {
								generallissimo
							}
						}
					}
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = neutrality
					long_name = QIN_neutrality_restoration_party_long
					name = QIN_neutrality_restoration_party
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_war_support = 0.75
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = CHI
					}
					add_core_of = QIN
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_claimed_by = CHI
					}
					add_claim_by = QIN
				}
				load_oob = "QIN_restoration"
				set_rule = {
					can_join_factions = no
				}
				add_ideas = standing_alone	
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = CHI
				type = annex_everything
			}
			change_tag_from = ROOT
		}
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
	}
}

# DEATH OF YUAN SHIKAI
#########################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.10
	title = ww1_china.10.t
	desc = {
		text = ww1_china.10.d
		trigger = { NOT = { country_exists = QIN } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ww1_china.10.d2
		trigger = { country_exists = QIN }
	}
	picture = QIN_report_event_qing_funeral
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					country_exists = QIN
					country_exists = CHI
				}
			}
			is_china_or_warlord = yes
			owns_state = 608
		}
		else = {
			has_character = CHI_yuan_shikai
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				CHI = { exists = yes }
				date > 1916.5.1
			}
			date > 1917.8.1
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 35
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_yuan_shikai
				}
				retire_character = CHI_yuan_shikai
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = yuan_shikai_dead }
				}
				CHI = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_completed_focus = CHI_ruling_of_yuan_shikai }
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = {
									has_completed_focus = CHI_second_empire
								}
							}
							remove_ideas = CHI_idea_republican_plot
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { has_global_flag = hongxian_failed }
							}
							CHI_beiyang_triumvirate = {
								add_country_leader_role = {
									promote_leader = yes
									country_leader = {
										ideology = oligarchism
										desc = CHI_beiyang_triumvirate_desc
										traits = { CHI_beiyang_triumvirate }
									}
								}
								add_country_leader_role = {
									promote_leader = yes
									country_leader = {
										ideology = stratocracy
										desc = CHI_beiyang_triumvirate_desc
										traits = { CHI_beiyang_triumvirate }
									}
								}
							}
							CHI_duan_qirui = {
								set_can_be_fired_in_advisor_role = {
									slot = political_advisor
									value = no
								}
							}
							activate_advisor = CHI_duan_qirui_political
							CHI_feng_guozhang = {
								set_can_be_fired_in_advisor_role = {
									slot = political_advisor
									value = no
								}
							}
							activate_advisor = CHI_feng_guozhang_political
							CHI_wang_shizhen = {
								set_can_be_fired_in_advisor_role = {
									slot = political_advisor
									value = no
								}
							}
							activate_advisor = CHI_wang_shizhen_political
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_government = neutrality
								has_elections = yes
							}
							set_politics = {
								ruling_party = neutrality
								election_frequency = 60
								elections_allowed = no
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_idea = CHI_idea_hongxian_emperor
						}
						remove_ideas = CHI_idea_hongxian_emperor
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_idea = CHI_idea_stable_republic
						}
						swap_ideas = {
							remove_idea = CHI_idea_stable_republic
							add_idea = CHI_idea_unstable_republic
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = yuan_shikai_dead
			set_global_flag = yuan_shikai_dead
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_china_or_warlord = yes
					NOT = { has_country_flag = yuan_shikai_dead }
				}
				set_country_flag = yuan_shikai_dead
				country_event = ww1_china.10
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.10.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			retire_character = CHI_yuan_shikai
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = QIN
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = -0.15
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.11
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		GZC = {
			exists = no
		}
		has_global_flag = warlord_era
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
	}
	immediate = {
		every_possible_country = {
			limit = {
				has_character = CHI_liu_xianshi
			}
			CHI_liu_xianshi = {
				set_nationality = GZC
			}
		}
		GZC = {
			CHI_liu_xianshi = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = { ideology = despotism }
				}
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = { ideology = stratocracy }
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_china_or_warlord = yes
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 603
						}
					}
					add_core_of = GZC
					GZC = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = {
						has_character = CHI_liu_xianshi
					}
					CHI_liu_xianshi = {
						set_nationality = GZC
					}
				}
				load_oob = CHI_warlord
				capital_scope = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"JuntuÃ¡n\"	start_experience_factor = 0.4	start_equipment_factor = 1"
						owner = PREV
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						count = 2
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = QIN
					}
					inherit_technology = QIN
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 5000
						producer = QIN
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_tech = tech_support
						}
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = support_equipment
							amount = 500
							producer = QIN
						}
					}
					QIN = {
						add_to_faction = PREV
					}
					else = {
						inherit_technology = CHI
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = infantry_equipment
							amount = 5000
							producer = CHI
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_tech = tech_support
							}
							add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
								type = support_equipment
								amount = 500
								producer = CHI
							}
						}
						CHI = {
							set_truce = {
								target = PREV
								days = 330
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.14
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		SHX = {
			exists = no
		}
		OR = {
			country_exists = ANC
			has_global_flag = qing_oppress_cliques
		}
		has_global_flag = warlord_era
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 35
	}
	immediate = {
		SHX = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_china_or_warlord = yes
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 615
						}
					}
					add_core_of = SHX
					SHX = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no

				}
			}

				}

						promote_leader = yes

							ideology = conservatism
							traits = { king_shanxi propaganda_expert }
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_ideology = stratocracy
					}
					promote_character = stratocracy
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = stratocracy
							traits = { king_shanxi propaganda_expert }
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy
					}
					promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = authoritarian_democracy
							traits = { king_shanxi propaganda_expert }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			load_oob = CHI_warlord
			capital_scope = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "division_template = \"JuntuÃ¡n\"	start_experience_factor = 0.4	start_equipment_factor = 1"
					owner = PREV
					allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					count = 10
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = ANC
						original_tag = ZHC
					}
				}
				PREV = { give_military_access = PREV }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = QIN
				}
				inherit_technology = QIN
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = 5000
					producer = QIN
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_tech = tech_support
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = support_equipment
						amount = 500
						producer = QIN
					}
				}
				QIN = {
					add_to_faction = PREV
				}
				else = {
					inherit_technology = ANC
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 5000
						producer = ANC
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_tech = tech_support
						}
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = support_equipment
							amount = 500
							producer = ANC
						}
					}
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = ANC
						relation = military_access
						active = yes
					}
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = ZHC
						relation = military_access
						active = yes
					}
					every_other_country = {
						limit = {
							is_neighbor_of = PREV
						}
						set_truce = {
							target = PREV
							days = 365
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.16
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		FNG = {
			exists = no
		}
		has_global_flag = warlord_era
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 5
	}
	immediate = {
		SIK = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_china_or_warlord = yes
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 287
							state = 618
							state = 749
							state = 894
						}
					}
					add_core_of = SIK
					SIK = {
						transfer_state = PREV
						every_owned_state = {
							set_demilitarized_zone = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_china_or_warlord = yes
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 619
						}
					}
					add_core_of = KUM
					KUM = {
						transfer_state = PREV
						every_owned_state = {
							set_demilitarized_zone = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
			982 = {
				add_claim_by = SIK
				if = {
					limit = {
						owner = { is_china_or_warlord = yes }
					}
					330 = {
						owner = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									is_china_or_warlord = no
								}
								transfer_state = 982
							}
							else = {
								SIK = { transfer_state = 982 }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = {
						has_character = CHI_yang_zengxin
					}
					CHI_yang_zengxin = {
						set_nationality = SIK
					}
				}
				CHI_yang_zengxin = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = { ideology = despotism traits = { stout_defender } }
					}
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = { ideology = stratocracy traits = { stout_defender } }
					}
				}
				load_oob = CHI_warlord
				capital_scope = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"JuntuÃ¡n\"	start_experience_factor = 0.4	start_equipment_factor = 1"
						owner = PREV
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						count = 4
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = QIN
					}
					inherit_technology = QIN
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 5000
						producer = QIN
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_tech = tech_support
						}
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = support_equipment
							amount = 500
							producer = QIN
						}
					}
					QIN = {
						add_to_faction = PREV
					}
					else = {
						inherit_technology = CHI
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = infantry_equipment
							amount = 5000
							producer = CHI
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_tech = tech_support
							}
							add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
								type = support_equipment
								amount = 500
								producer = CHI
							}
						}
						get_current_government_type = yes
						CHI = {
							set_autonomy = {
								target = PREV
								autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_regional_government
							}
						}
						restore_previous_government_type = yes
					}
				}
				KUM = { get_current_government_type = yes }
				set_autonomy = {
					target = KUM
					autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet
				}
				KUM = { restore_previous_government_type = yes }
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

								ideology = reformist_socialism

							}
						}
					}
				}

						}
					}
					every_possible_country = {
						limit = {
							has_character = CHI_sun_yatsen
						}
						CHI_sun_yatsen = {
							set_nationality = JNC
						}
					}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.20
	title = ww1_china.20.t
	desc = ww1_china.20.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers
	trigger = {
		tag = ZHC
		has_global_flag = second_zhili_fengtian_war_end
		has_war = no
		NOT = {
			owns_state = 608 #Beijing
			country_exists = JNC
		}
		OR = {
			owns_state = 598
			owns_state = 606
			owns_state = 613
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			JNC = {
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = { has_character = ZHC_qi_xieyuan }
					ZHC_qi_xieyuan = {
						promote_leader = yes
						set_nationality = JNC
					}
				}
				ZHC_qi_xieyuan = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = despotism
						}
					}
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = stratocracy
						}
					}
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						owner = { is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes }
						OR = {
							state = 598
							state = 606
							state = 613
						}
					}
					remove_core_of = ROOT
					add_core_of = PREV
					transfer_state_to = PREV
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					set_demilitarized_zone = no
				}
				inherit_technology = ZHC
				set_truce = {
					target = ZHC
					days = 365
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = fascism
					long_name = ZHC_neutrality_party
					name = ZHC_neutrality_party
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = neutrality
					long_name = ZHC_neutrality_party
					name = ZHC_neutrality_party
				}
				# add_ideas = CHI_idea_beiyang_army
				# add_ideas = CHI_idea_reorganized_military_industry
				# add_ideas = CHI_idea_chinese_unity
				# add_ideas = CHI_idea_local_military_development3
				ZHC = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_army_size = {
								size > 20
							}
						}
						transfer_units_fraction = {
							target = PREV
							size = 0.15
							air_ratio = 0
							navy_ratio = 0
							keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
								always = yes
							}
						}
					}
					set_truce = {
						target = PREV
						days = 365
					}
				}
				division_template = {
					name = "Jiangxujun"
					division_names_group = CHI_INF_02
					regiments = {
						infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
						artillery_brigade = { x = 0 y = 3 }
						infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
						artillery_brigade = { x = 1 y = 3 }
						infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
						infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }
						artillery_brigade = { x = 2 y = 3 }
						infantry = { x = 3 y = 0 }
						infantry = { x = 3 y = 1 }
						infantry = { x = 3 y = 2 }
						cavalry = { x = 4 y = 0 }
						cavalry = { x = 4 y = 1 }
						cavalry = { x = 4 y = 2 }
					}
					support = {
						engineer = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_army_size = { size < 12 }
					}
					capital_scope = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "division_template = \"Jiangxujun\"	start_experience_factor = 0.7	start_equipment_factor = 1"
							owner = PREV
							allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
							count = 7
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.20.a
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.20.b
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		JNC = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
	}

			}

		}

		NOT = { country_exists = ANC }
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	immediate = {

			if = {

					is_in_faction = yes

				}

					set_nationality = ANC

				limit = {

					set_nationality = ANC

				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_duan_zhigui
				}
				CHI_duan_zhigui = {
					set_nationality = ANC
				}
			}

				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_feng_guozhang

					set_nationality = ZHC
				}

				limit = {

				}

					set_nationality = ZHC

			}

				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_du_xigui

					set_nationality = ZHC
				}
			}
			ANC = {
				CHI_duan_qirui = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_ideology = oligarchism
						}
						promote_character = oligarchism
					}
					else = {

							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = { ideology = oligarchism }
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_ideology = stratocracy
						}
						promote_character = stratocracy
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = { ideology = oligarchism }
						}
					}
				}
				load_oob = CHI_warlord
				inherit_technology = CHI
				set_research_slots = 3
				annex_country = {
					target = CHI
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
				add_ideas = CHI_idea_warlord_neutrality
				if = {
					limit = {
						CHI = { has_idea = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_president }
					}
					meta_effect = {
						text = {
							set_politics = {
								ruling_party = neutrality
								last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
								election_frequency = 60
								elections_allowed = no
							}
						}
						CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
					}
					add_ideas = CHI_idea_xu_shichang_president
					else = {
						add_ideas = CHI_idea_xu_shichang_president
					}
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = CHI
						is_core_of = QIN
					}
				}
				add_core_of = ANC
				# STOP RELEASE DAMN CHINA
				remove_core_of = CHI
				remove_core_of = QIN
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_claimed_by = CHI
						is_claimed_by = QIN
					}
				}
				add_claim_by = ANC
				remove_claim_by = CHI
				remove_claim_by = QIN
			}
			ZHC = {
				CHI_cao_kun ={
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_ideology = oligarchism
						}
						promote_character = oligarchism
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = { ideology = oligarchism }
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_ideology = stratocracy
						}
						promote_character = stratocracy
					}
					else = {

					}
					else = {

							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = { ideology = oligarchism }
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_ideology = stratocracy
						}
						promote_character = stratocracy
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = { ideology = oligarchism }
						}
					}
				}
				inherit_technology = CHI
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OWNER = {
							is_china_or_warlord = yes
							OR = {
								is_subject = no
								AND = {
									is_subject = yes
									OVERLORD = { is_china_or_warlord = no }
								}
							}
						}
						OR = {
							#Zhili
							state = 614
							#Shandong
							state = 597
							state = 872
							#Henan
							state = 607
							state = 891

							state = 598
							#Hubei
							state = 620
							#Jiangxi
							state = 600
						}
					}
					add_core_of = PREV
					transfer_state_to = PREV
				}
				add_ideas = CHI_idea_warlord_neutrality
				every_owned_state = {
					set_demilitarized_zone = no
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_china_or_warlord = yes
						NOT = { has_war_with = PREV }
					}

						target = PREV
						days = 365
					}
				}

							region = 143

							region = 164
						}
					}
					teleport_armies = {
						limit = {
							tag = ZHC
						}
						to_state = 614
					}
				}
			}
			ANC = {
				transfer_units_fraction = {

					size = 0.5
					stockpile_ratio = 0.5

				target = ROOT
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 65
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_major = yes
			}

				factor = 0.1
				OR = {
					tag = XSM
					tag = SHX
					tag = GXC
					tag = SIK
					tag = YUN
					tag = SCC
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio > 0.5
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < 70
				}
			}
		}
	}

		name = ww1_china.31.b

			country_event = ww1_china.32
		}

			base = 35

# UNITED CHINA - SHARE PROBLEMS WITH WARLORDS

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.35
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		is_chinese_warlord = yes
		NOT = { has_country_flag = part_of_china }
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = MAN
			}
			NOT = { is_subject_of = JAP }
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	immediate = {
		add_ideas = CHI_idea_warlord_neutrality
		set_country_flag = part_of_china
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_subject = yes
				OVERLORD = { has_country_flag = part_of_china }
			}
			copy_warlord_problem = yes
			add_ideas = CHI_ineffective_bureaucracy_warlord
			add_ideas = PRC_government_corruption
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_illiteracy
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_weak_industry
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_idea = CHI_idea_inflation5
						has_idea = CHI_idea_inflation4
						has_idea = CHI_idea_inflation3
						has_idea = CHI_idea_inflation2
						has_idea = CHI_idea_inflation
					}
				}
				add_ideas = CHI_idea_inflation5
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_idea = CHI_idea_army_corruption3
						has_idea = CHI_idea_army_corruption2
						has_idea = CHI_idea_army_corruption
					}
				}
				add_ideas = CHI_idea_army_corruption
			}
			add_ideas = CHI_ineffective_bureaucracy_warlord
			add_ideas = PRC_government_corruption
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_illiteracy
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_weak_industry

			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_idea = MAN_banditry
						has_idea = CHI_idea_merchant_army
					}
				}
				add_ideas = CHI_banditry
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						num_of_factories > 4
						tag = FNG
						tag = GXC
						tag = ANC
						tag = ZHC
					}
				}
				add_ideas = CHI_rampant_opiate_addiction
			}
		}
	}
}

			NOT = { original_tag = ANC }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ww1_china.42.e
		trigger = {
			original_tag = ANC
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting
	# trigger = {
	# 	original_tag = ZHC
	# 	country_exists = ANC
	# 	OR = {
	# 		has_global_flag = zhili_anhui_war
	# 		has_war_with = ANC
	# 	}
	# 	NOT = {
	# 		has_global_flag = zhili_anhui_war_end
	# 		has_global_flag = first_zhili_fengtian_war
	# 		has_global_flag = second_zhili_fengtian_war
	# 		has_global_flag = zhili_fengtian_fengyushang_war
	# 		has_global_flag = zhili_fengtian_fengyushang_war_end
	# 		has_global_flag = northern_expedition
	# 	}
	# }

	# mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.42.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { original_tag = ANC }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = first_zhili_fengtian_war }
			}
			set_global_flag = zhili_anhui_war
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_war_with = ANC }
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = ANC
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
				add_to_war = {
					targeted_alliance = ROOT
					enemy = ANC
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				FNG = {
					country_event = ww1_china.42
				}
				ANC = {
					country_event = ww1_china.42
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.42.b
		trigger = { original_tag = ANC }
		custom_effect_tooltip = ww1_china.42.b.tt
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.43
	title = ww1_china.43.t
	desc = ww1_china.43.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_officers
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			ANC = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = CHI_idea_xu_shichang_president
					}
					remove_ideas = CHI_idea_xu_shichang_president
					ZHC = { add_ideas = CHI_idea_xu_shichang_president }
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
							AND = {
								is_subject = yes
								OVERLORD = { is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes }
							}
						}
						has_war_with = PREV
					}
					set_country_flag = zhili_anhui_war_victor
					white_peace = PREV
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						FNG = { has_country_flag = zhili_anhui_war_victor }
					}
					transfer_units_fraction = {
						target = FNG
						size = 0.3
						keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
							always = yes
						}
					}
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								# to event
								# state = 606
								# state = 607
								# state = 891
								state = 609
								state = 610
								state = 611
								state = 612
								state = 983
							}
						}
						transfer_state_to = FNG
					}
				}
				transfer_units_fraction = {
					target = ZHC
					size = 0.6
					keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
						always = yes
					}
				}
				CHI_xu_shichang = {
					set_nationality = ZHC
				}
				ANC_li_houji = {
					set_nationality = ZHC
				}
				transfer_navy = {
					target = ZHC
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							state = 329
							state = 330
							state = 595
							state = 596
							state = 613
							state = 622
							state = 982
							state = 983
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = ZHC
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = SHN
					}
					ZHC = { transfer_state = 890 }
					#Yu Youren
					SHN = {
						PREV = { end_puppet = PREV }
						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = democratic
							elections_allowed = no
						}
					}
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							region = 143
							region = 144
							region = 164
						}
					}
					teleport_armies = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								tag = ANC
								is_in_faction_with = ANC
								is_subject_of = ANC
							}
						}
						to_state = 613
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_army_size = { size < 10 }
					}
					division_template = {
						name = "Zhejiangjun"
						division_names_group = CHI_INF_02
						regiments = {
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
							artillery_brigade = { x = 0 y = 3 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
							artillery_brigade = { x = 1 y = 3 }
							infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }
							artillery_brigade = { x = 2 y = 3 }
							infantry = { x = 3 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 3 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 3 y = 2 }
							cavalry = { x = 4 y = 0 }
							cavalry = { x = 4 y = 1 }
							cavalry = { x = 4 y = 2 }
						}
						support = {
							engineer = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						}
					}
					capital_scope = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "division_template = \"Zhejiangjun\"	start_experience_factor = 0.7	start_equipment_factor = 1"
							owner = PREV
							allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
							count = 10
						}
					}
				}
			}
			ZHC = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
					dismantle_faction = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ANC = { has_character = HNC_zhang_jingyao }
					}
					HNC_zhang_jingyao = { set_nationality = ZHC }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = XSM
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						owner = { is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes }
						OR = {
							state = 283
							state = 616
							# state = 621
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = XSM
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = PREV
					owner = {
						is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = no
					}
				}
				add_core_of = ZHC
				remove_core_of = PREV
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = PREV
				}
				add_claim_by = ZHC
				remove_claim_by = PREV
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = ANC
						has_country_flag = zhili_anhui_war_victor
					}
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tag = ANC
							has_country_flag = zhili_anhui_war_victor
						}
					}
					set_truce = {
						target = PREV
						days = 365
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = ww1_china.44
					days = 3
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = zhili_anhui_war_end
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.43.a
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.47
	title = ww1_china.47.t
	desc = ww1_china.47.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting

		has_global_flag = second_constitutional_protection_movement
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			GDC = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = democratic
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				set_popularities = {
					democratic = 32
					neutrality = 65
					fascism = 0
					communism = 3
				}
				set_capital = {
					state = 592
				}

							ideology = despotism
						}

							ideology = stratocracy
						}

					}
				}
			}

					has_character = CHI_chen_jiongming

					set_nationality = KMT

				}

				}

					set_nationality = KMT
				}

					NOT = { state = 599 }
				}
				add_core_of = GDC

							is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
						}
						OR = {
							state = 592
							state = 892

				}

			KMT = {
				unlock_national_focus = CHI_secure_internal_politics
				unlock_national_focus = CHI_focus_align_with_guangzhou_government
				unlock_national_focus = CHI_cooperation_with_the_nationalists

				# unlock_national_focus = CHI_focus_government_divided
				# unlock_national_focus = CHI_focus_guangxi
				# unlock_national_focus = CHI_focus_cp_movement
				if = {
					limit = {

					}
					inherit_technology = GXC
					else = {
						inherit_technology = CHI
					}
				}
				set_party_name = {

					long_name = CHI_kuomintang_party_long
					name = CHI_kuomintang_party
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = communism

					name = CHI_left_kuomintang_party

				}
				set_stability = 0.9
				set_war_support = 0.7
				add_ideas = CHI_idea_constitutional_movement
				add_ideas = CHI_idea_sun_yatsen_president_2

							has_global_flag = sun_yatsen_dead
						}

					}
					CHI_sun_yatsen = {
						if = {
							limit = { has_ideology = tridemism }
							promote_character = tridemism
						}
						else = {

									ideology = tridemism
									traits = { chinese_nationalist father_of_the_republic }
								}
								promote_leader = yes
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						CHI_wang_jingwei = {
							if = {
								limit = { has_ideology = tridemism }
								promote_character = tridemism
							}
							else = {
								add_country_leader_role = {
									promote_leader = yes
									country_leader = {
										ideology = tridemism
										traits = { chinese_nationalist }
									}
								}
							}
							if = {
								limit = { has_ideology = reformist_socialism }
								promote_character = reformist_socialism
							}
							else = {
								add_country_leader_role = {
									promote_leader = yes
									country_leader = {
										ideology = reformist_socialism
										traits = { chinese_nationalist }
									}
								}
							}
						}
						CHI_hu_hanmin = {
							if = {
								limit = { has_ideology = tridemism }
								promote_character = tridemism
							}
							else = {
								add_country_leader_role = {
									country_leader = {
										ideology = tridemism
										traits = { conservative_nationalist }
									}
									promote_leader = yes
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				CHI_chen_jiongming = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = social_liberalism
							traits = { chinese_federalist decentralist_liberal }
						}
					}
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = authoritarian_democracy
							traits = { chinese_federalist decentralist_liberal }
						}
					}
					add_country_leader_role = {

# DEATH OF SUN YAT-SEN
#########################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.54
	title = ww1_china.54.t
	desc = {
		text = ww1_china.54.d
		trigger = { has_global_flag = xinhai_revolution }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ww1_china.54.d_alt
		trigger = { NOT = { has_global_flag = xinhai_revolution } }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_europe_funeral
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		has_character = CHI_sun_yatsen
		date > 1925.3.1
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 12
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_sun_yatsen
				}
				retire_character = CHI_sun_yatsen
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag
						has_character = CHI_hu_hanmin
					}
					CHI_hu_hanmin = {
						if = {
							limit = { has_ideology = tridemism }
							promote_character = tridemism
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								country_leader = {
									ideology = tridemism
									traits = { conservative_nationalist }
								}
								promote_leader = yes
							}
						}
					}
					suspend_elections = yes
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = sun_yatsen_dead
			set_global_flag = sun_yatsen_dead
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_china_or_warlord = yes
					NOT = { has_country_flag = sun_yatsen_dead }
				}
				set_country_flag = sun_yatsen_dead
				country_event = ww1_china.54
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.54.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			retire_character = CHI_sun_yatsen
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag }
				promote_character = CHI_hu_hanmin
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = democratic
				has_government = communism
				has_country_leader_ideology = authoritarian_democracy
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.54.b
		effect_tooltip = {
			retire_character = CHI_sun_yatsen
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = democratic
				has_government = communism
				has_country_leader_ideology = authoritarian_democracy
			}
		}
	}
}

# COMMUNIST PARTY OF CHINA

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.57
	title = ww1_china.57.t
	desc = ww1_china.57.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_gathering_protest
	trigger = {
		date > 1919.1.1
		is_china_or_warlord = yes
		OR = {
			country_exists = SOV
			has_global_flag = october_revolution
			has_global_flag = french_civil_war
			has_global_flag = CHI_may_fourth_movement
			any_other_country = {
				is_major = yes
				has_government = communism
			}
			communism > 0.50 #manual override
		}
		NOT = {
			has_government = communism
			has_global_flag = chinese_communist_party
		}
		# on chinese mainland
		capital_scope = {
			OR = {
				region = 143
				region = 144
				region = 164
				region = 165
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 100 }
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = chinese_communist_party
			set_country_flag = chinese_communist_party
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = 0.05
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = CHI_idea_communist_movement
				days = 365
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_leader_ideology = anarchist_communism
						has_country_leader_ideology = syndicalism
						has_global_flag = french_civil_war
					}
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = communism
					long_name = CHI_syndicalist_party_long
					name = CHI_syndicalist_party
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = communism
					long_name = CHI_communist_party_long
					name = CHI_communist_party
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_china_or_warlord = yes
					NOT = {
						original_tag = PRC
						has_country_flag = chinese_communist_party
						has_government = communism
					}
				}
				country_event = ww1_china.57
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_li_dazhao
				}
				CHI_li_dazhao = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						# promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = vanguardism
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_government = communism } }
					CHI_li_dazhao = { promote_character = vanguardism }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.57.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = communism }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.57.b
		trigger = {
			has_government = communism
		}
	}
}

# CHINESE SOVIET REPUBLIC

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.58
	title = ww1_china.58.t
	desc = ww1_china.58.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_gathering_protest
	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = chinese_communist_party
		has_global_flag = warlord_era
		is_china_or_warlord = yes
		NOT = {
			has_government = communism
			has_global_flag = chinese_soviet_republic
			any_country = {
				has_idea = CHI_idea_united_front
			}
			any_country = {
				is_china_or_warlord = yes
				has_government = communism
			}
		}
		owns_state = 600
		any_owned_state = {
			is_chinese_core = yes
			NOT = { state = 600 }
		}
		OR = {
			date > 1931.11.1
			has_global_flag = northern_expedition_end
			communism > 0.3
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = chinese_soviet_republic
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = CHI_idea_communist_movement
				}
				remove_ideas = CHI_idea_communist_movement
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = CHI_idea_united_front
				}
				remove_ideas = CHI_idea_united_front
			}
			PRC = {
				add_state_core = 600
				transfer_state = 600

				# set_cosmetic_tag = CSR

				set_rule = { can_join_factions = no }
				capital_scope = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"JuntuÃ¡n\"	start_experience_factor = 0.4	start_equipment_factor = 1"
						owner = PREV
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes

					}
				}
				news_event = ww1_china.107

				set_country_flag = part_of_china
				add_ideas = CHI_idea_warlord_neutrality
				add_ideas = CHI_ineffective_bureaucracy_warlord
				add_ideas = PRC_government_corruption
				add_ideas = CHI_idea_illiteracy
				add_ideas = CHI_idea_weak_industry
				add_ideas = CHI_banditry
				add_ideas = CHI_rampant_opiate_addiction
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.58.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = -0.10
		}
		CSR = {
			every_neighbor_country = {
				limit = {
					is_china_or_warlord = yes
					NOT = {
						has_government = communism
						is_in_faction_with = PREV
						is_subject_of = PREV
					}
				}
				PREV = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = PREV
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
		}
		#add_civil_war_target = CSR
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.58.b
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = -0.10
		}
		CSR = {
			every_neighbor_country = {
				limit = {
					is_china_or_warlord = yes
					NOT = {
						has_government = communism

# END OF NORTHERN EXPEDITION
#########################################
news_event = {
	id = ww1_china.61
	title = ww1_china.61.t
	desc = ww1_china.61.d
	major = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_news_event_chinese_street
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = northern_expedition_end }
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_war_with = KMT
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								tag = ZHC
								tag = JNC
								tag = ANC
							}
						}
						transfer_navy = {
							target = KMT
						}
						KMT = {
							annex_country = {
								target = PREV
								transfer_troops = yes
							}
						}
						every_state = {
							limit = {
								OR = {
									is_core_of = PREV
									is_claimed_by = PREV
								}
							}
							remove_core_of = PREV
							remove_claim_by = PREV
						}
					}
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							OR = {

country_event = {

	desc = ww1_china.64.d

		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_china_or_warlord = yes

				}
				white_peace = KMT
			}
			KMT = {
				annex_country = {
					target = GMJ
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_core_of = GMJ
							is_claimed_by = GMJ
						}
					}
					remove_core_of = GMJ
					remove_claim_by = GMJ
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_owned_by = SHX

						}
						OR = {
							state = 608
							state = 609
							state = 611
							state = 612
							state = 614
							state = 983
						}
					}
					add_core_of = PREV
					transfer_state_to = PREV

					state = 598
				}
			}
			SHX = {

					target = KMT
					days = 300
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
					dismantle_faction = yes
				}
				set_capital = {
					state = 615
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = PREV
						NOT = {
							is_owned_by = PREV
						}
					}
					remove_core_of = PREV
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_claimed_by = PREV
					}
					remove_claim_by = PREV
				}
			}
			GXC = {
				set_truce = {
					target = KMT
					days = 300
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = PREV
						NOT = {
							is_owned_by = PREV
						}
					}
					remove_core_of = PREV
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_claimed_by = PREV
					}
					remove_claim_by = PREV
				}
			}
			FNG = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = KMT
					}
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								is_owned_by = SHX
								is_owned_by = GXC
								is_owned_by = KMT
							}
							OR = {
								state = 608

							}
						}
						add_core_of = PREV
						transfer_state_to = PREV
					}
					set_truce = {
						target = KMT
						days = 300
					}
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = PREV
							NOT = {

							}
						}
						remove_core_of = PREV
					}
					KMT = {
						give_guarantee = PREV
					}

			}

# MANCHURIAN INCIDENT
#########################################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.65
	title = ww1_china.65.t
	desc = ww1_china.65.t
	is_triggered_only = yes
	# trigger = {
	# 	OR = {
	# 		has_country_flag = reunited_china
	# 		has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag
	# 		AND = {
	# 			tag = SHX
	# 			has_global_flag = anti_chiang_war
	# 			has_cosmetic_tag = CHI_united
	# 		}
	# 	}
	# 	is_in_faction_with = FNG
	# 	JAP = {
	# 		has_war_with = FNG
	# 	}
	# }
	# mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	# fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			GXC = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_global_flag = anti_chiang_war
						has_cosmetic_tag = KMT_GUANGZHOU
					}
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = warlord_era_end
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = reunite_china
						country_exists = CHI
					}
					any_country = {
						has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag
					}
				}
				KMT = {
					add_to_faction = FNG
					set_country_flag = manchurian_incident
				}
				FNG = {
					add_to_war = {
						targeted_alliance = KMT
						enemy = JAP
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = anti_chiang_war
					SHX = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = CHI_united
					}
				}
				SHX = {
					add_to_faction = FNG
					set_country_flag = manchurian_incident
				}
				FNG = {
					add_to_war = {
						targeted_alliance = SHX
						enemy = JAP
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = reunite_china
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = reunited_china
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_country_flag = CHI_soviet_republic_flag
								has_country_flag = CHI_left_kuomintang_flag
								has_country_flag = long_march_end
								has_cosmetic_tag = KMT_BEIPING
								has_cosmetic_tag = QIN_government
								has_government = communism
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								is_faction_leader = yes
							}
							set_faction_name = chinese_salvation_army
							else = {
								create_faction = chinese_salvation_army
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_government = communism
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								is_faction_leader = yes
							}
							set_faction_name = chinese_red_army
							else = {
								create_faction = chinese_red_army
							}
						}
					}
					add_to_faction = FNG
					set_country_flag = manchurian_incident
					FNG = {
						add_to_war = {
							targeted_alliance = PREV
							enemy = JAP
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.65.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.66
	title = ww1_china.66.t
	desc = ww1_china.66.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = tanggu_truce }
				}
				set_global_flag = tanggu_truce
				# FNG = {
				# 	if = {
				# 		limit = {
				# 			has_war_with = FROM
				# 		}
				# 		transfer_navy = {
				# 			target = ROOT
				# 		}
				# 		transfer_units_fraction = {
				# 			target = ROOT
				# 			size = 0.3
				# 			keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
				# 				always = yes
				# 			}
				# 		}
				# 	}
				# }
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_war_with = FROM
							has_war_with = MAN
						}
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_china_or_warlord = yes
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
					white_peace = FROM
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						609 = { owner = { is_china_or_warlord = yes } }
					}
					609 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							OR = {
								is_china_or_warlord = yes
								original_tag = JAP
								is_subject_of = JAP
							}
						}
						OR = {
							state = 611
							state = 612
							state = 983
						}
					}
					# Inner Mongolia
					##################################
					MEN = {
						add_state_core = PREV
						transfer_state = PREV
						add_popularity = {
							ideology = fascism
							popularity = 0.3
						}
						add_ideas = fascist_influence
						JAP = {
							diplomatic_relation = {
								country = PREV
								relation = non_aggression_pact
								active = yes
							}
							diplomatic_relation = {
								country = PREV
								relation = guarantee
								active = yes
							}
						}
						every_other_country = {
							limit = {
								is_neighbor_of = ROOT
								owns_state = 608
							}
							diplomatic_relation = {
								country = PREV
								relation = non_aggression_pact
								active = yes
							}
							diplomatic_relation = {
								country = PREV
								relation = guarantee
								active = yes
							}
						}
						set_rule = {
							can_join_factions = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.66.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.66.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		FROM = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = ROOT
				type = puppet_wargoal_focus
			}
		}
	}
}

# TANG JIYAO IS OVERTHROWN
###########################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.67
	title = ww1_china.67.t
	desc = ww1_china.67.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_detained_china
	trigger = {
		tag = YUN
		OR = {
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = CHI_cooperation_with_the_nationalists
					has_cosmetic_tag = YUN_KMT
				}
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = northern_expedition
					any_other_country = {
						is_kuomintang_state = yes
						has_country_flag = reunited_china
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				any_enemy_country = {
					is_kuomintang_state = yes
				}
				surrender_progress > 0.3
			}
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.67.a
		hidden_effect = {
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_tang_jiyao
				}
				retire_character = CHI_tang_jiyao
			}
			YUN_long_yun = {
				promote_character = conservatism
				promote_character = stratocracy
				promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = YUN_KMT
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			every_enemy_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_kuomintang_state = yes
						AND = {
							is_subject = yes
							OVERLORD = {
								is_kuomintang_state = yes
							}
						}
						AND = {
							is_in_faction = yes
							any_allied_country = {
								is_kuomintang_state = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
				white_peace = ROOT
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 603 }
				599 = {
					owner = {
						transfer_state = 603
					}
				}
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag
				}
				ROOT = { get_current_government_type = yes }
				set_autonomy = {
					target = ROOT
					autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_regional_government
				}
				ROOT = { restore_previous_government_type = yes }
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			YUN_long_yun = {
				promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
			}
		}
	}
}

# DEATH OF FENG GUOZHANG
###########################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.68
	title = ww1_china.68.t
	desc = {
		text = ww1_china.68.d
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				country_exists = CHI
				AND = {
					country_exists = ZHC
					country_exists = ANC
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ww1_china.68.d2
		trigger = {
			NOT = { country_exists = CHI }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ww1_china.68.d3
		trigger = {
			any_country = {
				has_idea = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_president
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_funeral
	trigger = {
		date > 1919.4.1
		has_character = CHI_feng_guozhang
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 12 }
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_feng_guozhang
				}
				retire_character = CHI_feng_guozhang
			}
			set_country_flag = feng_guozhang_dead
			set_global_flag = feng_guozhang_dead
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_china_or_warlord = yes
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = feng_guozhang_dead
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = feng_guozhang_dead
				country_event = ww1_china.68
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.68.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			retire_character = CHI_feng_guozhang
		}
		add_political_power = -75
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_president
			}
			remove_ideas = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_president
			set_country_flag = duan_qirui_president
			set_country_flag = chinese_government_crackdown
			meta_effect = {
				text = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = ROOT
						last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
						election_frequency = 60
						elections_allowed = yes
					}
				}
				CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				# prepare government divide
				ANC = {
					meta_effect = {
						text = {
							set_politics = {
								ruling_party = neutrality
								last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
								election_frequency = 60
								elections_allowed = no
							}
						}
						CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
					}
					# Duan is president, no need to add ideas
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

# END OF ANTI-CHIANG WAR (BEIPING VICTORY)
#############################################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.69
	title = ww1_china.69.t
	desc = ww1_china.69.t
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_china_or_warlord = yes
				has_war_with = KMT
			}
			white_peace = KMT
		}
		SHX = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = KMT
				}
				add_core_of = SHX
				remove_core_of = KMT
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = KMT
				}
				add_claim_by = SHX
				remove_claim_by = KMT
			}
			KMT = {
				every_unit_leader = {
					set_nationality = PREV.PREV
				}
				transfer_navy = {
					target = PREV
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = PREV
					}
					remove_core_of = PREV
					add_core_of = SHX
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_claimed_by = PREV
					}
					remove_claim_by = PREV
					add_claim_by = SHX
				}
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = KMT
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			set_capital = {
				state = 608
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = KMT_BEIPING
			set_truce = {
				target = FNG
				days = 300
			}
			add_to_faction = FNG
			set_global_flag = warlord_era_end
			change_tag_from = KMT
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.69.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

			}
		}
		HNC = {
			leave_faction = yes

				target = ROOT
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
	}
}

# WANG JINGWEI AND GUANGZHOU GOVERNMENT
##########################################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.72
	title = ww1_china.72.t
	desc = ww1_china.72.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_officers
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.72.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CHI_idea_constitutional_movement }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = CHI_idea_constitutional_movement
				add_idea = CHI_idea_nationalist_revolution
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = reunited_china
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 598
				}
				hidden_effect = { set_capital = { state = 598 } }
				set_cosmetic_tag = KMT_NANJING
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 620
				}
				hidden_effect = { set_capital = { state = 620 } }
				set_cosmetic_tag = KMT_WUHAN
			}
			else = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = KMT_GUANGZHOU
			}
		}
		CHI_wang_jingwei = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = tridemism }
				promote_character = tridemism
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = tridemism
						traits = { chinese_nationalist }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		CHI_chiang_kaishek = {
			promote_leader = yes
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy }
				promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democracy
						traits = { chinese_nationalist generallissimo }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = neutrality
			long_name = CHI_revolutionary_army_long
			name = CHI_revolutionary_army
		}
	}
}

				}

				limit = { has_ideology = conservatism }
				promote_character = conservatism
			}

			elections_allowed = no
		}

			ideology = neutrality

		}

		show_ideas_tooltip = CHI_hu_hanmin

	}

# ZHANG JINGYAO IS OVERTHROWN
################################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.74
	title = ww1_china.74.t
	desc = ww1_china.74.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_detained_china
	trigger = {
		original_tag = HNC
		has_country_leader = {
			character = HNC_zhang_jingyao
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		country_exists = ANC
		country_exists = ZHC
		NOT = { has_government = fascism }
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 900
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.74.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_subject = yes
				OVERLORD = { is_china_or_warlord = yes }
			}
			OVERLORD = {
				end_puppet = PREV
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						has_war_with = PREV
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
					white_peace = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		HNC_zhang_jingyao = {
			remove_country_leader_role = {
				ideology = despotism
			}
			remove_country_leader_role = {
				ideology = stratocracy
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 0.5
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = 0.4
			}
			CHI_zhao_hengti = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy
					}
					promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = {
								ideology = authoritarian_democracy
								traits = { chinese_federalist }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_ideology = social_liberalism
					}
					promote_character = social_liberalism
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = {
								ideology = social_liberalism
								traits = { chinese_federalist }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			608 = {
				owner = {
					ROOT = {
						HNC_zhang_jingyao = {
							set_nationality = PREV.PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
			CHI_zhao_hengti = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_trait = chinese_nationalist
					}
					remove_unit_leader_trait = chinese_nationalist
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = democratic
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			promote_character = HNC_tan_yankai
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = democratic
				long_name = CHI_zhigong_party_long
				name = CHI_zhigong_party
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			CHI_zhao_hengti = {
				promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
			}
		}
	}
}

# National Assembly refuses to join the war!
