country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.81
	title = ww1_china.81.t
	desc = ww1_china.81.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_parliament
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		has_idea = CHI_idea_li_duan_conflict
		has_global_flag = duan_qirui_great_war
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	# Send Zhang Xun to Beijing
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.81.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = historical_tt
		add_stability = 0.05
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_china.146
				days = 3
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
	# Side with Li Yuanhong
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.81.b
		hidden_effect = {
			promote_character = CHI_li_yuanhong
			remove_ideas = CHI_idea_duan_qirui
			remove_ideas = CHI_idea_li_duan_conflict
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				dismantle_faction = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = FNG
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 328
							state = 717
						}
					}
					add_core_of = FNG
					transfer_state_to = FNG
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
		start_civil_war = {
			ideology = fascism
			size = 0.5
			states = {
				595
				596
				597
				872
				606
				607
				609
				610
				611
				614
				617
				619
				716
				872
			}
			keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
				NOT = {
					is_character = QIN_zhang_xun
					is_character = CHI_duan_qirui
				}
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = ANC
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = neutrality
				long_name = CHI_neutrality_anfu_party
				name = CHI_neutrality_anfu_party
			}
			PREV = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = li_yuanhong_in_charge
					}
					PREV = {
						transfer_units_fraction = {
							target = PREV
							size = 0.2
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				democratic > 0.40
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				fascism < 0.05
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

# DEATH OF CAI E
###########################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.82
	title = ww1_china.82.t
	desc = ww1_china.82.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_funeral
	trigger = {
		date > 1916.11.1
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { country_exists = CHI }
			}
			NOT = { original_tag = QIN }
			is_china_or_warlord = yes
			owns_state = 608
		}
		else = {
			has_character = CHI_cai_e
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 8 }
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_cai_e
				}
				retire_character = CHI_cai_e
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					has_country_flag = CHI_national_protection_flag
				}
				CHI_tang_jiyao = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = stratocracy }
						promote_character = stratocracy
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								ideology = stratocracy
							}
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy }
						promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								ideology = authoritarian_democracy
							}
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
				CHI_liang_qichao = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = reformist_socialism }
						promote_character = reformist_socialism
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								ideology = reformist_socialism
								traits = { gentle_scholar }
							}
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = conservatism }
						promote_character = conservatism
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								ideology = conservatism
								traits = { gentle_scholar }
							}
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = cai_e_dead
			set_country_flag = cai_e_dead
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_china_or_warlord = yes
					NOT = { has_country_flag = cai_e_dead }
				}
				set_country_flag = cai_e_dead
				country_event = ww1_china.82
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.82.a
		add_political_power = -75
	}
}

# CHINISE UNITED FRONT IN WARLORD ERA
########################################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.83
	title = ww1_china.83.t
	desc = ww1_china.83.d
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = QIN
			tag = CHI
			AND = {
				OR = {
					tag = ANC
					tag = ZHC
					tag = FNG
				}
				owns_state = 608
			}
			has_country_flag = reunited_china
		}
		is_subject = no
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = warlord_era_end
		}
		OR = {
			is_faction_leader = yes
			is_in_faction = no
		}
		OR = {
			any_other_country = {
				is_china_or_warlord = no
				is_major = yes
				NOT = { tag = SIK }
				NOT = { tag = MON }
				NOT = { tag = TIB }
				has_offensive_war_with = PREV
			}
			AND = {
				any_other_country = {
					is_china_or_warlord = yes
					is_subject = no
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = PREV
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							PREV = {
								has_government = communism
							}
						}
						has_government = communism
						else = {
							NOT = {
								has_government = communism
							}
						}
					}
					any_other_country = {
						is_china_or_warlord = no
						is_major = yes
						has_offensive_war_with = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.83.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		# FLAGS
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = chinese_salvation_army
			set_country_flag = chinese_salvation_army_leader
		}
		# CREATE FACTION
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = no
			}
			create_faction = chinese_salvation_army
			else = {
				hidden_effect = {
					set_country_flag = chinese_salvation_army_reserve
				}
				set_faction_name = chinese_salvation_army
			}
		}
		# INVITE OTHER CHINESE COUNTRIES
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				is_china_or_warlord = yes
				is_subject = no
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = PREV
					is_in_faction_with = PREV
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						PREV = {
							has_government = communism
						}
					}
					has_government = communism
					else = {
						NOT = {
							has_government = communism
						}
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = ww1_china.84
		}
		# GOOD EFFECTS
		add_war_support = 0.1
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.83.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

# CHINA IS AT WAR AGAINST GERMANY IN WARLORD ERA
###################################################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.89
	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = warlord_era
		OR = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					tag = CHI
					tag = QIN
				}
				OR = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
					AND = {
						is_in_faction = no
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = warlord_era
						}
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				is_china_or_warlord = yes
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = reunited_china
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
		}
		is_subject = no
		NOT = {
			is_in_faction_with = GER
			has_global_flag = great_war_ends
			has_war_with = FRA
			is_in_faction_with = FRA
		}
		OR = {
			has_war_with = GER
			GER = {
				has_completed_focus = GER_chinese_intervention
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	fire_only_once = yes
	hidden = yes
	immediate = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = PREV
				NOT = {
					is_subject_of = PREV
					is_in_faction_with = GER
					has_war_with = FRA
					is_in_faction_with = FRA
				}
			}
			FRA = {
				add_to_faction = PREV
			}
		}
		FRA = {
			add_to_faction = PREV
		}
	}
}

# Fate of Guo Songling
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.102
	title = ww1_china.102.t
	desc = ww1_china.102.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_officers
	trigger = {
		tag = FNG
		owns_state = 608
		OR = {
			GMJ = {
				has_war_with = ROOT
				NOT = { has_government = communism }
			}
			any_enemy_country = {
				is_kuomintang_state = yes
				is_subject = no
				NOT = { has_government = communism }
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 70
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.102.a
		trigger = {
			JAP = {
				is_neighbor_of_subject = yes
				is_subject = no
				NOT = {
					has_government = communism
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 75
		retire_character = FNG_guo_songling
		remove_ideas = CHI_FNG_idea_regionalist_sentiment
		add_ideas = CHI_FNG_idea_kwantung_army
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.102.b
		add_political_power = -75
		remove_ideas = CHI_FNG_idea_regionalist_sentiment
		effect_tooltip = {
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = democratic
				size = 0.3
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = democratic
				size = 0.3
				keep_political_leader = yes
				keep_political_party_members = yes
				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
					NOT = { has_trait = chinese_nationalist }
				}
				set_country_flag = part_of_china
				ROOT = {
					FNG_guo_songling = {
						set_nationality = PREV.PREV
					}
				}
				FNG_guo_songling = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = { ideology = authoritarian_democracy }
					}
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = { ideology = conservatism }
					}
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = { ideology = stratocracy }
					}
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
						OR = {
							is_kuomintang_state = yes
							tag = GMJ
							is_subject = no
						}
					}
					PREV = { get_current_government_type = yes }
					set_autonomy = {
						target = PREV
						autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_regional_government
						end_wars = no
						end_civil_wars = no
					}
					PREV = { restore_previous_government_type = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

# Shanghai Massacre
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.103
	title = ww1_china.103.t
	desc = ww1_china.103.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting
	trigger = {
		has_country_leader = {
			character = CHI_chiang_kaishek
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		613 = { is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_ally = yes }
		has_global_flag = chinese_communist_party
		OR = {
			has_idea = CHI_idea_united_front
			communism > 0.10
		}
		has_capitulated = no
		is_subject = no
		has_country_flag = wuhan_government
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.103.a
		set_global_flag = shanghai_massacre
		clr_country_flag = wuhan_government
		set_country_flag = nanjing_government
		set_cosmetic_tag = KMT_NANJING
		598 = { set_state_owner_to = ROOT }
		set_capital = { state = 598 }
		CHI_wang_jingwei = {
			set_nationality = HNC
		}
		HNC = {
			hidden_effect = {
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = democratic
					long_name = CHI_left_kuomintang_party
					name = CHI_left_kuomintang_party
				}
				ROOT = { end_puppet = PREV }
			}
			set_country_flag = wuhan_government
			set_cosmetic_tag = KMT_WUHAN
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
						NOT = { tag = PREV }
					}
					OR = {
						state = 620
						AND = {
							controller = {
								is_kuomintang_state = yes
							}
							OR = {
								state = 600
								state = 602
								state = 893
							}
						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = PREV
			}
			set_capital = { state = 620 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = CHI_idea_communist_movement
			}
			remove_ideas = CHI_idea_communist_movement
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = CHI_idea_united_front
			}
			remove_ideas = CHI_idea_united_front
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = -0.30
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_other_country = {
						has_country_leader = {
							character = CHI_li_dazhao
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				retire_character = CHI_li_dazhao
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = {
						has_character = CHI_li_dazhao
					}
					retire_character = CHI_li_dazhao
				}
			}
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				is_major = yes
				has_government = communism
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = large_decrease
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = communism
				long_name = CHI_left_kuomintang_party
				name = CHI_left_kuomintang_party
			}
			news_event = {
				id = ww1_china.104
				hours = 3
			}
		}
	}
}

# Presidential Problem
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.113
	title = ww1_china.113.t
	desc = ww1_china.113.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_officers
	is_triggered_only = yes
	# Side with Duan Qirui
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.113.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			promote_character = CHI_duan_qirui
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = neutrality
				size = 0.5
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = CHI_idea_duan_qirui
			remove_ideas = CHI_idea_li_duan_conflict
			remove_ideas = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_president
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				dismantle_faction = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = FNG
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						owner = { is_china_or_warlord = yes }
						OR = {
							state = 328
							state = 717
						}
					}
					add_core_of = FNG
					transfer_state_to = FNG
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_china_or_warlord = yes
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				ROOT = { end_puppet = PREV }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = SIK
					country_exists = KUM
				}
				SIK = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = KUM
						autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet
					}
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = neutrality
				long_name = CHI_neutrality_anfu_party
				name = CHI_neutrality_anfu_party
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = neutrality
				size = 0.35

	desc = ww1_china.117.d

	fire_only_once = yes

		tag = CHI
		has_global_flag = national_protection_war
		has_capitulated = no
		NOT = {
			has_government = democratic
			has_government = communism
		}
		any_other_country = {
			original_tag = CHI
			has_war_with = PREV
			has_country_flag = CHI_national_protection_flag
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = lu_rongting_npa
				ROOT = { surrender_progress > 0.30 }
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 30 }

		name = ww1_china.117.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = historical_tt

			remove_unit_leader_trait = yuan_shikai_loyalist
		}
		CHI_feng_guozhang = {
			remove_unit_leader_trait = yuan_shikai_loyalist
		}

				id = ww1_china.118
				days = 10
			}
		}

			factor = 0
		}
	}

# Cai E Restores Democracy 
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.122
	title = ww1_china.122.t
	desc = ww1_china.122.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_officers
	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		has_global_flag = national_protection_war
		has_country_flag = CHI_national_protection_flag
		NOT = {
			has_government = communism
			has_government = fascism
			has_country_flag = lu_rongting_npa
			has_global_flag = hongxian_failed
		}
		has_war = no
		is_subject = no
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.122.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = {
				character = CHI_cai_e
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
		remove_ideas = standing_alone
		set_cosmetic_tag = NPA_government
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = chinese_communist_party }
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = communism
				long_name = QIN_progressive_party_long
				name = QIN_progressive_party
			}
			CHI_liang_qichao = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_ideology = reformist_socialism }
					promote_character = reformist_socialism
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							ideology = reformist_socialism
							traits = { gentle_scholar }
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		CHI_liang_qichao = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = conservatism }
				promote_character = conservatism
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						ideology = conservatism
						traits = { gentle_scholar }
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
			
		}
		meta_effect = {

# REQUEST WEIHAIWEI
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.124
	title = ww1_china.124.t
	desc = {
		text = ww1_china.124.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				original_tag = ENG
				is_subject_of = ENG
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ww1_china.124.d
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = ENG
				is_subject_of = ENG
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.124.a
		FROM = { transfer_state = 746 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_government = fascism
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				any_other_country = {
					is_china_or_warlord = yes
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				any_other_country = {
					is_china_or_warlord = yes
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_war_with = JAP
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < 0
				}
			}
		}
	}

			base = 10

				add = -5
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -5
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 30
				}
			}

				add = -5

					ratio < 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# DEATH OF HUANG XING

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.129
	title = ww1_china.129.t
	desc = ww1_china.129.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_europe_funeral
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { country_exists = CHI }
			}
			is_china_or_warlord = yes
			owns_state = 608
		}
		else = {
			has_character = CHI_huang_xing
			NOT = { original_tag = QIN }
		}
		date > 1916.10.1
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 31
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_huang_xing
				}
				retire_character = CHI_huang_xing
			}
			set_country_flag = huang_xing_dead
			set_global_flag = huang_xing_dead
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_china_or_warlord = yes
					NOT = { has_country_flag = huang_xing_dead }
				}
				set_country_flag = huang_xing_dead
				country_event = ww1_china.129
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.129.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			retire_character = CHI_huang_xing
		}
	}
}

# End of Beiyang Triumvirate
## This for when Yuan Shikai died without declaring the empire
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.131
	title = ww1_china.131.t
	desc = ww1_china.131.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_officers
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.131.a
		retire_character = CHI_beiyang_triumvirate
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 60
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
		CHI_duan_qirui = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = oligarchism }
				promote_character = oligarchism
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						ideology = oligarchism
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = stratocracy }
				promote_character = stratocracy
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						ideology = stratocracy
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
		}
		CHI_li_yuanhong = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = oligarchism }
				promote_character = oligarchism
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						ideology = oligarchism
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
		}
		set_rule = {
			can_not_declare_war = yes
			can_join_factions = no
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			CHI_duan_qirui = {
				set_can_be_fired_in_advisor_role = {
					slot = political_advisor
					value = yes
				}
			}
			CHI_feng_guozhang = {
				set_can_be_fired_in_advisor_role = {
					slot = political_advisor
					value = yes
				}
			}
			CHI_wang_shizhen = {
				set_can_be_fired_in_advisor_role = {
					slot = political_advisor
					value = yes
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = chinese_warlord_crisis
			set_global_flag = warlord_era
			country_event = ww1_china.2
			retire_character = CHI_yuan_keding
			set_capital = { state = 608 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = sun_yatsen_dead
					}
				}
				CHI_sun_yatsen = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = tridemism }
						promote_character = tridemism
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								ideology = tridemism
								traits = { chinese_nationalist father_of_the_republic }
							}
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_popularities = {
				democratic = 40
				neutrality = 50
				fascism = 8
				communism = 2
			}
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_duan_qirui
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_vice_president
			unlock_national_focus = CHI_beiyang_meditator
		}
		country_event = {
			id = ww1_china.98
			days = 10
		}
	}
}

			}
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				democratic > 0.60
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

# Li Yuanhong restores democracy
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.145
	title = ww1_china.145.t
	desc = ww1_china.145.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SWI_assembly_hall
	trigger = {
		has_country_leader = {
			character = CHI_li_yuanhong
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		has_government = neutrality
		has_civil_war = no
		is_subject = no
		NOT = {
			has_idea = CHI_idea_li_duan_conflict
			has_idea = CHI_idea_duan_qirui
			has_global_flag = constitutional_protection_war
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.145.a
		add_stability = 0.10
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				neutrality > 30
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 60
				neutrality > 60
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 80
				neutrality > 80
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.145.b
		add_stability = 0.10
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = democratic
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		# Li Yuanhong clique transfered to democratic
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.30
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = CHI_idea_beiyang_government }
				remove_ideas = CHI_idea_beiyang_government
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = CHI_idea_beiyang_government2 }
				remove_ideas = CHI_idea_beiyang_government2
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = neutrality
				long_name = CHI_neutrality_progressive_party
				name = CHI_neutrality_progressive_party
			}
			CHI_li_yuanhong = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = conservatism
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				democratic > 10
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				democratic > 30
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 60
				democratic > 60
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 80
				democratic > 80
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

# Li Yuanhong Presidency ended
## This is needed when if the Great War is over before Duan's demand to join the war
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.153
	title = ww1_china.153.t
	desc = ww1_china.153.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.153.a
		hidden_effect = {
			ANC = {
				meta_effect = {
					text = {
						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = neutrality
							last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
							election_frequency = 60
							elections_allowed = no
						}
					}
					CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
				}
				# Duan is president, no need to add ideas
			}
			set_country_flag = chinese_government_crackdown
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = feng_guozhang_dead }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_vice_president
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_vice_president
					add_idea = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_president
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_president
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = CHI_idea_duan_qirui
			}
			remove_ideas = CHI_idea_duan_qirui
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = CHI_idea_li_duan_conflict
			}
			remove_ideas = CHI_idea_li_duan_conflict
		}
		CHI_duan_qirui = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = oligarchism }
				promote_character = oligarchism
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						ideology = oligarchism
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
		}
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = ROOT
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 60
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
	}
}

# NPA Victorious
##############################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.154
	title = ww1_china.154.t
	desc = ww1_china.154.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_china_infiltration
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			CHI = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				set_popularities = {
					democratic = 31
					neutrality = 63
					fascism = 4
					communism = 2
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = neutrality
					long_name = CHI_national_protection_army_long
					name = CHI_national_protection_army
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = fascism
					long_name = CHI_national_protection_army_long
					name = CHI_national_protection_army
				}
				NPA = {
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								is_core_of = PREV
								is_claimed_by = PREV
							}
						}
						remove_core_of = PREV
						remove_claim_by = PREV
					}
					transfer_navy = {
						target = CHI
					}
					every_unit_leader = {
						set_nationality = CHI
					}
					CHI_cai_e = {
						set_nationality = CHI
					}
					CHI_sun_yatsen = {
						set_nationality = CHI
					}
					CHI_tang_jiyao = {
						set_nationality = CHI
					}
					CHI_liang_qichao = {
						set_nationality = CHI
					}
				}
				annex_country = {
					target = NPA
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
				retire_character = CHI_yuan_shikai
				retire_character = CHI_yuan_keding
				every_unit_leader = {
					limit = {
						has_trait = yuan_shikai_loyalist
					}
					remove_unit_leader_role = yes
				}
				CHI_tang_jiyao = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy }
						promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								ideology = authoritarian_democracy
								traits = { chinese_federalist }
							}
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = stratocracy }
						promote_character = stratocracy
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								ideology = stratocracy
							}	
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_global_flag = cai_e_dead }
					}
					CHI_cai_e = {
						if = {
							limit = { has_ideology = revolutionary_nationalism }
							promote_character = revolutionary_nationalism
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								country_leader = {
									ideology = revolutionary_nationalism
									traits = {
										revolutionary_general
										generallissimo
									}
								}	
								promote_leader = yes
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy }
							promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								country_leader = {
									ideology = authoritarian_democracy
									traits = {
										revolutionary_general
										generallissimo
									}
								}	
								promote_leader = yes
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = { is_field_marshal = no }
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
				CHI_liang_qichao = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = conservatism }
						promote_character = conservatism
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								ideology = conservatism
								traits = { gentle_scholar  }
							}
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_global_flag = sun_yatsen_dead }
					}
					CHI_sun_yatsen = {
						if = {
							limit = { has_ideology = tridemism }
							promote_character = tridemism
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								country_leader = {
									ideology = tridemism
									traits = { chinese_nationalist father_of_the_republic }
								}
								promote_leader = yes
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_ideology = reformist_socialism }
							promote_character = reformist_socialism
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								country_leader = {
									ideology = reformist_socialism
									traits = { chinese_nationalist father_of_the_republic }
								}
								promote_leader = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = NPA
				set_country_flag = CHI_national_protection_flag
				change_tag_from = NPA
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.154.a
		remove_ideas = standing_alone
		add_stability = 0.10
	}
}

			}

	}

	id = ww1_china.158
	title = ww1_china.158.t
	desc = ww1_china.158.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.158.a
		FROM = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				is_china_or_warlord = yes
				has_war_with = FROM
			}
			ROOT = {
				add_to_war = {
					targeted_alliance = FROM
					enemy = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		add_ideas = CHI_idea_nationalist_revolution
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				has_country_leader_with_trait = chinese_nationalist
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_government = communism
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.158.b
		FROM = {
			create_wargoal = {
				target = ROOT
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				has_government = communism
			}
		}

	option = {
		name = ww1_china.170.a
		CHI = {
			annex_country = {
				target = TIB
				transfer_troops = no
			}
			add_manpower = -100000
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_equipment_1
				amount = -2500
				producer = CHI
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ENG = {
						is_in_faction_with = FRA
					}
				}
				CHI = {
					set_rule = {
						can_join_factions = yes
					}
				}
				FRA = {
					add_to_faction = CHI
				}
			}
			else = {
				CHI = {
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = ENG
						relation = guarantee
						active = yes
					}
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = ENG
						relation = non_aggression_pact
						active = yes
					}
				}
				ENG = {
						diplomatic_relation = {
						country = CHI
						relation = guarantee
						active = yes
					}
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = CHI
						relation = non_aggression_pact
						active = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.170.b
		CHI = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_china.171
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

# China - Question of the Constitution
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.174
	title = ww1_china.174.t
	desc = ww1_china.174.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_parliament
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.174.e
		custom_effect_tooltip = historical_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_idea = CHI_idea_yuan_constitution }
			}
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_yuan_constitution
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -25
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.174.a
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = CHI_idea_yuan_constitution
			add_idea = CHI_idea_monarchist_constitution
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_idea = CHI_idea_yuan_constitution }
			}
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_monarchist_constitution
		}
		CHI_popular_support_increase = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.174.b
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = CHI_idea_yuan_constitution
			add_idea = CHI_idea_military_constitution
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_idea = CHI_idea_yuan_constitution }
			}
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_military_constitution
		}
		CHI_army_support_increase = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.174.c
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = CHI_idea_yuan_constitution
			add_idea = CHI_idea_absolute_constitution
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_idea = CHI_idea_yuan_constitution }
			}
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_absolute_constitution
		}
		CHI_popular_support_decrease = yes
		CHI_army_support_decrease = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
	}

								CHI_trait_socialist_advocate
							}

		}
	}

# Tan Yankai Overthrown
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.181
	title = ww1_china.181.t
	desc = ww1_china.181.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_detained_china
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = HNC
		is_subject = no
		has_global_flag = warlord_era
		OR = {
			country_exists = ANC
			country_exists = ZHC
		}
		has_country_leader = {
			character = HNC_tan_yankai
			ruling_only = yes
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 180
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.181.a
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_leader_ideology = tridemism
			CHI_zhao_hengti = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy
					}
					promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = {
								ideology = authoritarian_democracy
								traits = { chinese_federalist }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_ideology = social_liberalism
					}
					promote_character = social_liberalism
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = {
								ideology = social_liberalism
								traits = { chinese_federalist }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			CHI_zhao_hengti = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_trait = chinese_nationalist
					}
					remove_unit_leader_trait = chinese_nationalist
				}
			}
			HNC_tan_yankai = {
				add_country_leader_trait = chinese_nationalist
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			elections_allowed = no
		}
	}
}

# Hunan Civil War
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.182
	title = ww1_china.182.t
	desc = ww1_china.182.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_city_ruin
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = HNC
		is_subject = no
		has_global_flag = warlord_era
		has_country_leader = {
			character = CHI_zhao_hengti
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		HNC_tan_yankai = {
			has_trait = chinese_nationalist
		}
		any_neighbor_country = {
			is_kuomintang_state = yes
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 180
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.182.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
				leave_faction = yes
			}
			check_democratic_civil_war_popularity = yes
			set_global_flag = hunan_civil_war
		}
		start_civil_war = {
			ideology = democratic
			size = civil_war_size_var
			states = { 893 }
			keep_political_leader = yes
			keep_political_party_members = yes
			keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = chinese_federalist
					has_trait = politically_connected
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = part_of_china
				PREV = {
					HNC_tan_yankai = {
						set_nationality = PREV.PREV
					}
				}
				promote_character = HNC_tan_yankai
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = democratic
					long_name = CHI_kuomintang_party_long
					name = CHI_kuomintang_party
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_zhao_hengti
				}
				CHI_zhao_hengti = { set_nationality = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Hunan Tang Shengzi

country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.185
	title = ww1_china.185.t
	desc = ww1_china.185.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting
	trigger = {
		tag = HNC
		has_character = HNC_tang_shengzhi
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader_with_trait = chinese_nationalist
		}
		any_neighbor_country = {
			is_kuomintang_state = yes
			has_war = yes
		}
		has_global_flag = northern_expedition
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.185.a
		remove_puppet_and_leave_faction = yes
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = neutrality
			long_name = CHI_kuomintang_party_long
			name = CHI_kuomintang_party
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = democratic
			long_name = CHI_kuomintang_party_long
			name = CHI_kuomintang_party
		}
		HNC_tang_shengzhi = {
			add_country_leader_role = {
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = conservatism
					traits = { chinese_nationalist }
				}
			}
			add_country_leader_role = {
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democracy
					traits = { chinese_nationalist }
				}
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		set_popularities = {
			democratic = 40
			neutrality = 60
		}
		KMT = {
			add_to_faction = ROOT
			effect_tooltip = {
				puppet = ROOT
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				ROOT = { get_current_government_type = yes }
				set_autonomy = {
					target = ROOT
					autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_regional_government
					end_wars = no
					end_civil_wars = no
				}
				every_enemy_country = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_war_with = ROOT
						}
					}
					ROOT = {
						add_to_war = {
							targeted_alliance = KMT
							enemy = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 602
			}
			620 = {
				owner = {
					set_state_controller = 602
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# The Chinese Troops Seize CER!
#################################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.187
	title = ww1_china.187.t
	desc = ww1_china.187.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_running
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.187.a
		FROM = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = CER
				type = annex_everything
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_china_or_warlord = yes
						OR = {
							is_in_faction_with = PREV
							is_subject_of = PREV
						}
					}
					add_to_war = {
						targeted_alliance = PREV
						enemy = CER
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_civil_war = yes
					has_capitulated = yes
					is_in_faction_with = FROM
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.187.b
		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				annex_country = {
					target = CER
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = RUS
						original_tag = SOV
					}
				}
				CER = {
					every_owned_state = {
						transfer_state_to = FROM
					}
				}
				annex_country = {
					target = CER
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				OR = {
					has_civil_war = yes
					has_capitulated = yes
					is_in_faction_with = FROM
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {

# Provisional Chief Executive
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.195
	title = ww1_china.195.t
	desc = ww1_china.195.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_parliament
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.195.a
		add_ideas = CHI_idea_duan_qirui_executive
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = ANC }
				ANC = {
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								is_core_of = ANC
								is_claimed_by = ANC
							}
						}
						remove_core_of = ANC
						remove_claim_by = ANC
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							country_exists = FNG
						}
						every_owned_state = {
							limit = {
								NOT = {
									state = 329
									state = 330
									state = 982
								}
							}
							transfer_state_to = FNG
						}
						transfer_units_fraction = {
							target = FNG
							size = 0.5
							keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
								always = yes
							}
						}
						transfer_navy = {
							target = FNG
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							country_exists = ZHC
						}
						transfer_units_fraction = {
							target = ZHC
							size = 1.0
							keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
								always = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
				annex_country = {
					target = ANC
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
			}
			# rest in peace
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = { has_character = ANC_xu_shuzheng }
				retire_character = ANC_xu_shuzheng
			}
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = { has_character = ANC_duan_zhigui }
				retire_character = ANC_duan_zhigui
			}
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = { has_character = ANC_ni_sichong }
				retire_character = ANC_ni_sichong
			}
			# move
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = { has_character = ANC_qu_tongfeng }
				ANC_qu_tongfeng = {
					set_nationality = ROOT
				}
			}
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = { has_character = ANC_wu_guangxin }
				ANC_wu_guangxin = {
					set_nationality = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Guangxi Overthrown
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.211
	title = ww1_china.211.t
	desc = ww1_china.211.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = GXC
		has_war = no
		is_subject = no
		is_kuomintang_state = no
		OR = {
			any_neighbor_country = {
				original_tag = GDC
				has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag
				any_enemy_country = {
					original_tag = GDC
					has_country_flag = CHI_zhigongdang_flag
				}
			}
			has_global_flag = yung_feng_incident
			has_global_flag = northern_expedition
		}
		OR = {
			has_government = neutrality
			has_government = fascism
		}
		has_character = GXC_li_zongren
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 40
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.211.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = historical_tt
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = CHI_lu_rongting }
			CHI_lu_rongting = {
				remove_country_leader_role = {
					ideology = despotism
				}
				remove_country_leader_role = {
					ideology = stratocracy
				}
				remove_unit_leader_role = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = CHI_chen_bingkun }
			CHI_chen_bingkun = {
				remove_unit_leader_role = yes
			}
		}
		retire_character = GXC_tan_haoming
		add_country_leader_trait = chinese_nationalist
		every_unit_leader = {
			limit = { has_trait = politically_connected }
			add_trait = {
				trait = chinese_nationalist
			}
		}
		set_party_name = { 
			ideology = neutrality 
			long_name = CHI_kuomintang_party_long
			name = CHI_kuomintang_party
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = GXC_KMT
		GXC_li_zongren = {
			promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
		}
		every_enemy_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_kuomintang_state = yes
					AND = {
						is_subject = yes
						OVERLORD = {
							is_kuomintang_state = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			white_peace = ROOT
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GXC_li_zongren = {
				promote_character = stratocracy
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_popularities = {
				democratic = 30
				neutrality = 60
				fascism = 0
				communism = 10
			}
			get_current_government_type = yes
		}
		KMT = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = ROOT
				autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_regional_government
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			restore_previous_government_type = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.211.b
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		retire_character = GXC_li_zongren
		retire_character = GXC_bai_chongxi
	}
}

# NPA denounces the Truce
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.215
	title = ww1_china.215.t
	desc = ww1_china.215.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_city_ruin
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.215.a
		hidden_effect = {
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_yuan_shikai
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_character = CHI_yuan_shikai
					}
					CHI_yuan_shikai = {
						set_portraits = {
							civilian = {
								large = "gfx/leaders/CHI/CHI_yuan_shikai.png"
							}
							army = {
								large = "gfx/leaders/CHI/CHI_yuan_shikai.png"
							}
						}
						set_character_name = CHI_yuan_shikai
						remove_country_leader_role = {
							ideology = oligarchism
						}
						remove_country_leader_role = {
							ideology = stratocracy
						}
						remove_unit_leader_role = yes
					}
				}
			}
			retire_character = CHI_yuan_keding
			set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_uprising
			set_capital = {
				state = 608
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = fascism
				long_name = CHI_fascism_party
				name = CHI_fascism_party
			}
			CHI_duan_qirui = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_unit_leader = yes
						is_field_marshal = no
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_ideology = oligarchism }
					promote_character = oligarchism
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							ideology = oligarchism
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_ideology = stratocracy }
					promote_character = stratocracy
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							ideology = stratocracy
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
			}
			CHI_li_yuanhong = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_ideology = oligarchism }
					promote_character = oligarchism
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							ideology = oligarchism
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
			}
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_unstable_republic
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			election_frequency = 60
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		set_popularities = {
			democratic = 40
			neutrality = 50
			fascism = 8
			communism = 2
		}
		set_rule = {
			can_not_declare_war = yes
		}
		add_ideas = CHI_idea_duan_qirui
		add_ideas = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_vice_president
		country_event = {
			id = ww1_china.98
			days = 10
		}
		set_stability = 0.30
		set_war_support = 0.25
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
}

# Chiang Kai-shek almost got killed
country_event = {
	id = ww1_china.222
	title = ww1_china.222.t
	desc = ww1_china.222.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_city_ruin
	trigger = {
		is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
		has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag
		has_character = CHI_chiang_kaishek
		CHI_chiang_kaishek = {
			OR = {
				is_leading_army = yes
				is_leading_army_group = yes
			}
		}
		has_global_flag = northern_expedition
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = northern_expedition_end
		}
		OR = {
			has_war_with = ZHE
			has_war_with = ZHC
		}
		any_state = {
			OR = {
				region = 144
				region = 164
			}
			owner = { has_war_with = ROOT }
			is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_ally = yes
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.222.a
		add_war_support = -0.10
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_china.222.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				surrender_progress > 0.10
				NOT = {
					has_country_leader = {
						character = CHI_chiang_kaishek
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_war_support = -0.30
		retire_character = CHI_chiang_kaishek
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = -0.10
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = democratic
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					communism > 0.15
					has_idea = CHI_idea_united_front
				}
			}
			CHI_wang_jingwei = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_ideology = tridemism
					}
					promote_character = tridemism
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = tridemism
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_ideology = reformist_socialism
					}
					promote_character = reformist_socialism
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = reformist_socialism
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			CHI_hu_hanmin = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_ideology = tridemism
					}
					promote_character = tridemism
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = tridemism
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy
					}
					promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = authoritarian_democracy
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader_with_trait = chinese_nationalist
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				add_to_faction = PREV
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = northern_expedition_end
			news_event = {
				id = ww1_china.61
				hours = 3
			}
		}
	}
}
